<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item
2.02.&#160; Results of Operations and
Financial Condition.</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160; On September 9, 2004, America&#146;s Car-Mart,
Inc. issued a press release announcing its first quarter operating results and
other information for the quarter ended July 31, 2004.&#160; A copy of the press release is attached hereto
as Exhibit 99.1 and incorporated herein by reference.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In accordance
with General Instruction B.2. for Form 8-K, the information contained in this
Item 2.02 and the exhibit hereto are being furnished and shall not be deemed to
be &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934,
as amended, or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section.&#160; The information contained in this Item 2.02
and the exhibit hereto shall not be deemed incorporated by reference in any
filing with the Securities and Exchange Commission under the Securities Act of
1933, as amended, or the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, whether
made before or after the date hereof and irrespective of any general
incorporation language in any filings.&#160; America&#146;s
Car-Mart, Inc. disclaims any intention or obligation to update or revise this
information.</font></p>

<div>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit
99.1</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h5 align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For Immediate Release</font></b></h5>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AMERICA&#146;S
CAR-MART REPORTS FIRST QUARTER EARNINGS OF $0.62 PER SHARE VS. FORECAST OF $.57
- - $.60</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">COMPANY
UPDATES EPS GUIDANCE FOR FISCAL 2005</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Bentonville, Arkansas
(September 9, 2004) &#150; </font></b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">America&#146;s
Car-Mart, Inc. (NASDAQ NMS: CRMT) today announced its operating results for the
first fiscal quarter ended July 31, 2004.&#160;
The Company&#146;s results are segmented into continuing and discontinued
operations.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Highlights
of first quarter operating results (continuing operations):</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Revenue growth of 17% compared to the
prior year quarter</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Income growth of 13% compared to the
prior year quarter</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Diluted EPS growth of 11% compared to the
prior year quarter</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.0in;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">&#149;</font><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Retail unit sales growth of 7% compared
to the prior year quarter</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
the three months ended July 31, 2004, revenues increased 17% to $50.8 million,
compared with $43.3 million in the same period of the prior fiscal year.&#160; Income for the quarter increased 13% to $4.9
million, or $0.62 per diluted share, versus $4.4 million, or $0.55 per diluted
share, in the same period last year.&#160;
Retail unit sales increased 7% to 6,461 vehicles in the current quarter,
compared to 6,066 vehicles in the same period last year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are pleased with our strong financial
results in the first quarter, including revenue growth of 17% and income growth
of 13% over the same period last year,&#148; commented T. J. (&#147;Skip&#148;) Falgout, III,
Chief Executive Officer of America&#146;s Car-Mart.&#160;
&#147;We continue to maintain an average retail sales price in the $7,000
range, consistent with our fourth fiscal quarter of last year, but well above
the approximately $6,400 average retail sales price we had a year ago at this
time.&#160; We believe that loans on these
higher-priced vehicles will perform better than loans on lower-priced
vehicles.&#160; At July 31, 2004, the
percentage of our accounts over 30 days past due was 3.4%, compared to 4.8% at
the same time last year.&#160; The decrease is
the result of the tighter delinquency standards we adopted in February.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#160;&#147;During the first quarter we opened two
dealerships in Texas, one in Sulphur Springs and the other in Corsicana.&#160; Since then we have opened our third
dealership this fiscal year in Marshall, Texas, bringing our total number of
dealerships to 73,&#148; stated Hank Henderson, America&#146;s Car-Mart&#146;s President.&#160; &#147;We plan to open eight new dealerships this
year, principally in Texas, Oklahoma and Missouri.&#160; We have been pleased with the results of our
new Texas dealerships and plan to continue our expansion in that market.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>


<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\JMS\nogwal\04-10519-1\task184522\10519-1-mm.htm',USER='nogwal',CD='Sep 14 11:31 2004' -->

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Fiscal 2005 Earnings Guidance</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company has updated its fiscal year 2005 earnings estimate from continuing
operations to take into account the actual results from the first quarter.&#160; Accordingly, the Company projects that it
will earn $2.27 to $2.36 per diluted share from continuing operations in FY
2005 as follows:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">Management will be holding a conference call on Thursday,

results.&#160; To participate, please dial
800-309-9490 (U.S. callers) or 706-634-0104 (International callers).&#160; Callers should dial in approximately 10
minutes before the call begins.&#160; The
conference call can also be accessed on </font></b>www.vcall.com<font style="font-weight:normal;">.&#160; A conference call
replay will be available one hour following the call for three days and can be
accessed by calling: 800-642-1687 (U.S. callers) or 706-645-9291 (International
callers), conference ID# 9697397.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">About America&#146;s Car-Mart</font></u></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">America&#146;s Car-Mart operates 73 automotive dealerships
in seven states and is the largest publicly held automotive retailer in the
United States focused exclusively on the &#147;Buy Here/Pay Here&#148; segment of the
used car market.&#160; The Company operates
its dealerships primarily in small cities throughout the South-Central United
States selling quality used vehicles and providing financing for substantially
all of its customers.&#160; For more
information on America&#146;s Car-Mart, please visit our website at
www.car-mart.com.</font></p>

forward-looking statements, including statements with respect to projected
earnings per share amounts and new dealership openings. Such forward-looking
statements are based upon management&#146;s current knowledge and assumptions.&#160; There are many factors that affect
management&#146;s view about future earnings and dealership openings. These factors
involve risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ
materially from management&#146;s present view. These factors include, without
limitation, assumptions relating to unit sales, average selling prices, credit
losses, gross margins, operating expenses, collection results, available real
estate and economic conditions, and other risk factors described under
&#147;Forward-Looking Statements&#148; of Item 1 of Part I of the Company&#146;s Annual Report
on Form 10-K for the fiscal year ended April 30, 2004 and its current and
